	function modificarCookieSeguimiento(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
	    var expires = "expires = "+d.toGMTString(); 
	    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + " ; " + expires+"; path=/; domain=.homecenter.com.co";
	}
  
  function getCookieInfoFinal(cname){
		var name = cname + "=";
    	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    	for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
        	var c = ca[i];
        	while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
        	if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    	}
    	return "";
	}
  
  function getCookieSeguimiento(cname){
      var name = cname + "=";
      var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
      for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
      return "";
    } 
  
  /*obtener  sku de producto desde la url*/	
	function $_GET(param){
		/* Obtener la url completa */
		url = document.URL;
		/* Buscar a partir del signo de interrogación ? */
		url = String(url.match(/\?+.+/));
		/* limpiar la cadena quitándole el signo ? */
		url = url.replace("?", "");
		/* Crear un array con parametro=valor */
		url = url.split("&");
		/*
		Recorrer el array url
		obtener el valor y dividirlo en dos partes a través del signo =
		0 = parametro
		1 = valor
		Si el parámetro existe devolver su valor
		*/
		x = 0;
		while (x < url.length)
		{
			p = url[x].split("=");
			if (p[0] == param)
			{
				return decodeURIComponent(p[1]);
			}
		x++;
		}
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $("#group").mouseover("mouseenter", function() {
            timer = setTimeout(function() {
                $("#group-content").show();
                $("#addBold").addClass("addBold");
            }, 350);
        });

        $("#group").on("mouseout", function() {
            clearInterval(timer);
        });

        $(".grupoSection").mouseleave(function() {
            $(".grupoSection").hide();
            $("#addBold").removeClass("addBold");

        });
    });
</script>

    /*
    You can use below ways to define rule.
    1. "checkName" : {"msg":"your error message"}.
    2. "checkName" : {"regex":"your regex expression","msg":"your error message"}.
    
    For 1, you should add the mapping into validator.funMapping, such as:
        validator.funMapping["your checkName"]= your check method for this check name.
    	validator.funMapping["test"]=validator.checkTest;
    	In the jsp, you can use it like this.  class="validate[test]"
    	
    For 2. You only need to use it in the jsp like this. class="custom[checkName]".
    
    For1 & 2, you can add a special error/success message render function. Sample:
        "required" : {
            (required)"msg" : "error message",
            (optional)"regex" : "your regex expression",
    		(optional)"succCall" : validator.requiredSuccCall,
    		(optional)"errorCall" : validator.requiredErrorCall
        }
    */

<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $(".caja-hot .lazy").one("load", function() {
            var parent = $(this).closest(".recomendado");
            //parent.find(".gradient").css({ opacity: 1, transition: "opacity 350ms ease" });
            parent.find(".preloader").removeClass("preloader-animation");
        }).each(function(image) {
            if (this.complete) {
                $(this).trigger("load");
            }
        });

        function lazyLoad() {

            // Tag img
            $('img[data-srcset]').each(function() {
                if ($(this).isInScene()) {
                    let imgUrl = $(this).attr('data-srcset');
                    $(this).removeAttr('data-srcset');
                    $(this).attr('srcset', imgUrl);
                    $(this).removeClass('hidden');
                }
            });

            // Tag Picture - source
            $('source[data-srcset]').each(function() {
                if ($(this).isInScene()) {
                    let imgUrl = $(this).attr('data-srcset');
                    $(this).removeAttr('data-srcset');
                    $(this).attr('srcset', imgUrl);
                    $(this).siblings('img').removeClass('hidden');
                }
            });
        }

        // Lazy load
        lazyLoad();
        $(document).scroll(function(e) {
            lazyLoad();
        });
    })

    // GESTURE //
    $.fn.extend({
        isInScene: function(arg) {
            arg = arg || {};
            arg.desfase = arg.desfase || 0;
            arg.desfase = parseInt(arg.desfase, 10);
            var pos_container = $(this).offset().top;
            var container_height = $(this).outerHeight();
            var pos_document = $(document).scrollTop();
            var window_height = $(window).height();
            return (pos_document + window_height > pos_container + arg.desfase && pos_container + container_height > pos_document + arg.desfase);
        }
    });
    $(document).scroll(function(e) {

        // Swipe gesture
        $(".gesture").each(function() {

            if ($(this).isInScene()) {
                $(this).addClass('ani-gesture');
            } else {
                $(this).removeClass('ani-gesture');
            }

        });


    });
</script>

<script>
    window.onload = function() {

        // Chatbot
        try {
			var siteC = document.cookie ? document.cookie.split(';') : '';
			var interno = false;
			var modulo = false;
			var pedroLabEnv = "";

			for (var i = 0; i < siteC.length; i++) {
				var cookie = siteC[i].trim().split('=');
				if (cookie[0] == 'NETSITE' && cookie[1] == 'interno') {
					interno = true;
				}
				if (cookie[0] == 'JSTOREID' && cookie[1] == 'pruebaPedro') {
					modulo = true;
				}
				if (cookie[0] == 'AVC_ENV') {
					pedroLabEnv = cookie[1];
				}
			}
			
			if (pedroLabEnv != "") { // Ambientes de prueba
				pedroLabEnv = pedroLabEnv.toLowerCase();
				switch (pedroLabEnv) {
					case "test":
						console.log('Initializing Widget V4 TEST...');
						$('footer').append("<script src='https://sodcoavcstoragetst.z20.web.core.windows.net/chatbot-imports.js'>");
						break;
					case "production":
						console.log('Initializing Widget V4 PRODUCTION...');
						$('footer').append("<script src='https://sodcoavcstorageprd.z20.web.core.windows.net/chatbot-imports.js'>");
						break;
					default:
						console.error("AVC Enviroment not implemented");
				}
			} else if (modulo) { // Módulo .com
				// ...
			}
			else {
				if (interno) { // Red interna
                    //BOT ANA Actual
					loadBotAnaActual();
				}
				else { // Internet
                    //BOT ANA Actual
					loadBotAnaActual();
				}
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("AVC ERROR: ", error);
		}

        function afterLoadEvents() {
            try {

                // JS Modal data tratment
                var autoriza = false;

                    if (autoriza === false) {
                        // Open autorization modal
                        e.preventDefault();
                        $('#abrirpopupautorizacion').trigger('click');

                });

                $('.autoriza').click(function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    autoriza = true;

                    $('form.footer-subscribe-form input[type="email"]').each(function(i, e) {
                        var email = $(e).val();
                        if (email !== '') {
                            var actionURL = $('form.footer-subscribe-form').eq(i).attr('action');
                            actionURL = actionURL.replace('https', 'http');
                            $('form.footer-subscribe-form').eq(i).attr('action', actionURL);
                            $('form.footer-subscribe-form').eq(i).submit();
                        }
                    })
                });

                $('.noautoriza').click(function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $('#closeButtonPopupHomeFooter').trigger('click');
                });

                //Marcación whatsapp business
                $('a[href*="https://api.whatsapp.com/send?phone=57320%205760081"]').click(() => {

            } catch (err) {
                console.log('Error footer-mobile.html');
            }
        }

        if (initRules) {
            initRules();
        }

    }

	function setRecommendation_Interaction(experimentId, recommendationId, sku, description, eventAction = "click") {
		var now = getDateTime();

		exponea.track("recommendation_interaction", {
			experiment_id: experimentId,
			recommendation_id: recommendationId,
			interaction_date: now,
			event: eventAction,
			sku: sku,
			description: description
		});
	};
	
	function getDateTime() {
		var current_datetime = new Date();
		
		var current_datetime_day = (current_datetime.getDate() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getDate() : current_datetime.getDate();
		var current_datetime_month = ((current_datetime.getMonth() +1) < 10) ? '0' + (current_datetime.getMonth() + 1) : current_datetime.getMonth() + 1;

		var current_datetime_hour = (current_datetime.getHours() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getHours() : current_datetime.getHours();
		var current_datetime_minute = (current_datetime.getMinutes() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getMinutes() : current_datetime.getMinutes();
		var current_datetime_second = (current_datetime.getSeconds() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getSeconds() : current_datetime.getSeconds();


		var dateTime = current_datetime.getFullYear() + "-" + current_datetime_month + "-" + current_datetime_day + " " + current_datetime_hour + ":" + current_datetime_minute + ":" + current_datetime_second;

		return dateTime;
	}

			versaQuantity += digitalData.ecom.productList[i].quantity + ",";
		}

		console.log('products = ', versaProducts);
		console.log('quantity = ', versaQuantity);

		console.log('metodo de envio = ', digitalData.ecom.shippingMethod);
		console.log('metodo de pago = ', digitalData.ecom.paymentMethod);

		versaTag.activityParams = {
			//Predefined parameters:
			"OrderID": digitalData.ecom.purchaseID,
			"Session": digitalData.page.sessionId,
			"Value": digitalData.ecom.TotalOrder,
			"productid": versaProducts,
			"productinfo": versaProducts,
			"Quantity": versaQuantity,
			//Custom parameters:
			"tipo_de_entrega": digitalData.ecom.shippingMethod,
			"forma_de_pago": digitalData.ecom.paymentMethod
		};
	} else {
		console.log('versatag pagina normal');
		versaTag.activityParams = {
			//Predefined parameters:
			"OrderID": "",
			"Session": "",
			"Value": "",
			"productid": "",
			"productinfo": "",
			"Quantity": "",
			//Custom parameters:
			"tipo_de_entrega": "",
			"forma_de_pago": ""
		};
	}
	//Static retargeting tags parameters. Syntax: "TagID1":"ParamValue1", "TagID2":"ParamValue2". ParamValue can be empty.
	versaTag.retargetParams = {};
	//Dynamic retargeting tags parameters. Syntax: "TagID1":"ParamValue1", "TagID2":"ParamValue2". ParamValue can be empty.
	versaTag.dynamicRetargetParams = {};
	// Third party tags conditional parameters and mapping rule parameters. Syntax: "CondParam1":"ParamValue1", "CondParam2":"ParamValue2". ParamValue can be empty.
	versaTag.conditionalParams = {};
	</script>

    //console.log('exponea login all pages imp cookie' + ca);
    var cookie_email = "EMAIL_ID=";
    for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);

  function eliminarCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
	    var expires = "expires = "+d.toGMTString(); 
	    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + " ; " + expires+"; path=/; domain=.homecenter.com.co";
	}
